=== Interpretation guide ===
1) best_fixed = one homogeneous learner assignment used at all sampled positions in the sequence.
2) local_then_joint = choose best assignment per position from isolated local interventions, then apply them jointly.
3) greedy_suffix_oracle = stronger sequence-level heterogeneous selector, chosen left-to-right using suffix NLL.
4) greedy_suffix_oracle is still not the exact omniscient global oracle over all position assignments.
5) If greedy_suffix_oracle beats best_fixed by a lot, that supports sequence-level heterogeneity strong enough to motivate selector architectures.
